1a1(1): rdo rje khros pa phur pa rtsa ba'i rgyud bzhugs so//
1b1(1): // rgya gar skad du/ badz+ra kro d+ha ki la ya mU la tan+t+ra/ bod skad du/ rdo rje khros pa phur pa rtsa ba'i rgyud/ bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje gzhon nu la phyag 'tshal lo// chos rnams skye ba
1b2(1): med pa la/ mnyam pa'i ngang la gnas shing / sgyu ma'i dpe brgyad ltar gnas pa la/ skye 'gag med cing bdag dang gzhan du ma mthong ste/ rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin dang / thams cad
1b3(1): byang chub sems gcig la/ snang ba tha dad par snang ste/ gcig dang du ma brjod las 'das/ kye kye/ byang chub sems kyi rang bzhin ni// ngo bo gcig las med pa la// gcig la
1b4(1): snang ba tha dad pas// gcig la du ma brjod las 'das// zhes gsungs so// dpe mnyam pa nyid dang // don mnyam pa nyid dang // thams cad lhun gyis grub pa nyid do// e ma ho//
2a1(1): 'khor ba mya ngan 'das pa'i chos// gcig dang du ma brjod las 'das// 'di zhes gcig tu bstan par dka'// 'khor ba nyid na mya ngan 'das// bcos slad med
2a2(1): par mya ngan 'das// zhes gsungs so// 'khor ba bcos bslad med rtogs na// yid bzhin nor bu dag 'dra ba'i// gang ltar byas kyang lhun gyis grub par yin par ston// dbye
2a3(1): ba med pa'i don rtogs so// byang chub sems kyi ngo bo ni// nam mkha' bzhin du brtag dka' zhing // ci yang med las cir yang snang // don dam kun rdzob gnyis su snang // gcig
2a4(1): dang tha dad du mar snang // 'khor ba nyid kyang mya ngan 'das// ma rig pa nyid yang dag lam// byang chub sems kyi don rtogs na// rtog pa g.yeng ba chos kyi sku// ma rig ye shes za
2b1(1): dad med// so sor snang ba phye ba tsam// ma rig pa yang lam du gcig/ dang po gang nas ma byung bas// tha ma gar yang 'gro ba med// dang po skye ba'i rgyu med pas// tha mar 'chi ba'i lam yang med// dngos po
2b2(1): gcig la mi gnas pas// 'di zhes gcig tu bstan du med// skye shi 'pho ba'i gnas med pas// gsad cing gcad la gzung du med// ma rig pa yi rtog pa yis// mi mthun bde sdug myong bar 'gyur// rdo rje lta/
2b3(1): bur gnas pa las// sgyu ma chu zla brag cha 'dra// zhes gsang ba'i tshig tu gsungs so// kye kye/ thugs rje chen po'i byin rlabs las// stong gsum rgyal ba'i skus gang yang // byang chub sems las g.yos pa
2b4(1): med// dper na nam mkha'i 'ja' tshon bzhin// dkar dmar sngo ste ngos bzung med// de bzhin sems kyi rang bzhin yang // 'di zhes gcig tu bstan du med// mi shes par snang 'ja' tshon 'dra// de phyir ma
2b5(1): bcos de bzhin bzhag/ ces rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu gsungs so// bde bar gshegs pa kun gyi gtso// yab yum sras bcas snang ba yang // byang chub sems kyi ngo bor gcig/ skye 'chi med pa'i byang chub
2b6(1): sems// 'du 'bral med do chos kyi sku// bzang ngan med do 'khor 'das chos// rgyu 'bras med do mnyam pa nyid// 'gag pa med pa'i sems nyid ni// dper na rmi lam sgyu ma 'dra// nam mkha' bzhin du ye
3a1(1): gnas la// nam mkha' 'di ni 'di 'dra zhes// tshig tu rab tu brjod du med// de bzhin sems kyi rang bzhin yang // 'di zhes gcig tu bstan du med// bstan na gzung 'dzin 'khrul pa'i
3a2(1): chos// bstan du med pa bstan pa'i mchog/ blta ru med pa blta ba'i mchog/ bsgom du med pa bsgom pa'i mchog/ bsrung du med pa'i dam tshig ni// ma bsrungs bzhin du lhun gyis grub// ma nor ma
3a3(1): bcos dbyings nyid las// rang bzhin lhun gyis grub pa'i dbyings// thog mar gzhal yas byang chub sems// de ni rgyu 'bras ma bkag chos// dper na rgya mtsho chen po la// chu bran thams cad 'bab cing
3a4(1): 'du// de bzhin byang chub sems nyid la// 'khor 'das gnyis ka 'byung zhing 'du// zhes rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu gsungs so// e ma bde gshegs snying po ni// nam mkha' bzhin du brtag dka' zhing // me
3a5(1): bzhin du gzung du med// brag cha bzhin du brjod dang bral// bcud kyi rdo rje snying po ni// bdag dang gzhan du dbye ru med// bstan du med pa'i chos nyid 'di// brjod du med kyis go bar
3a6(1): gyis// brjod med brjod pa rjod pa'i mchog/ mnyan bsam bsgom pa'i shes rab kyis// blo yi rtog pa kha phye nas// nges pa'i don 'di rtogs par gyis// nges pa'i don 'di ma rtogs na// bsgom pa bsgrub pa
3b1(1): yun ring yang // mi shes gzung 'dzin 'ching ba'i rgyu// de phyir rtogs pa sngon du 'gro// rtogs pa gdeng du ma gyur na// ji ltar bshad kyang 'ching ba'i rgyu// rtogs pa gdeng gi blta ba 'di// dngos po gshis kyi
3b2(1): gnas lugs brtag/ nges pa'i don 'di ma rtogs na// mnyam bzhag bsgoms kyang chags pa'i rgyu// spu gri'i nags tshal la sogs kyang // rang gi rtog pa brtas pa'i phyir// de phyir rtogs pa sngon du
3b3(1): btang // rab tu rtogs pa 'di zhes pas// rtogs pas brtags na kun kyang 'grub// rtogs pa'i don 'di rab tu gces// zhes de bzhin gshegs pa nyid la/ de bzhin gshegs pa nyid kyis ched du brjod
3b4(1): do// de nas 'og min gyi gnas mtha' dang dbus med pa/ rang bzhin gyi dur khrod chen po'i gnas na/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad til gyi gang bu bzhin gang bar gnas te/ bcom ldan 'das dur khrod kyi
3b5(1): bdag po zhes bya ba dang / gtso bo la 'khril ba'i yum dang / dregs pa can dbang du sdud pa'i 'jigs byed chen po bcu dang / 'khril ba'i yum dang / thogs pa med pa'i mgo brnyan dang / yang sbrul sum sprul
3b6(1): dpag tu med pa'i 'khor dang bcas nas/ rang bzhin gyis gnas so// de nas dur khrod kyi bdag po mnyam pa nyid la bzhugs nas 'di skad ces gsungs so// kye kye/ gtso bo gtso mo 'khor bcas
4a1(1): kyang // rang bzhin dur khrod chen po na// me long chu zla gzugs brnyan 'dra// nyon mongs dri mas gos pa med// rang bzhin don gyi dbyings na bzhugs// nam mkha'i cho 'phrul ston pa ste// rang
4a2(1): bzhin dur khrod dam pa na// gsung gi chos rnams mi ston te// thugs kyis chos rnams 'jal bar ston// thugs kyi brda' yis 'jal bar ston// zhes yum dang gnyis su med par mnyam par bzhugs so// rdo
4a3(1): rje khros pa rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ mnyam pa dang rtogs pa'i sgo nas gleng gzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o// // de nas yang dgyes pa chen po des 'og min gyi gnas na bzhugs nas// yum dang yang 'khril ba'i tshul du
4a4(1): gnas pa la/ kye kye/ dag pa dri ma med pa'i mchog/ bla med byang chub sgrub pa'i thabs// 'khor ba'i rnam rtogs sbyang ba dang // drag pos 'gro ba drang ba'i phyir// yab yum gnyis med 'khril ba'i tshul// zhes rdo
4a5(1): rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// de nas yul dang mnyam nyid 'khril ba'i tshul gyis/ kye kye/ bde gshegs rdo rje'i rigs kyi gtso// mnyam nyid chen po'i don bstan nas// gang la gang 'dul bstan pa'i phyir//
4a6(1): rigs kyi gtso mchog la// gnas med don gyis 'khyud par bgyi// zhes gsungs so// de nas yang dgyes pa chen pos gsang ba'i thugs mnyam pa'i ngang gis/ kye kye// don nyid snying po bde gshegs
4b1(1): gtso// bde gshegs thams cad thugs kyi sras// 'gro ba yongs kyi ded dpon gtso// gnyis su med pa'i yum dang bzhugs// zhes gleng bslangs te mi g.yo ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// de nas
4b2(1): yab yum chen mo nyid kyis mi g.yo ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas// kye kye/ bde bar gshegs pa kun gyi gtso// ma rig mun pa 'joms pa'i bdag/ kun kyang 'gro ba'i don bya'i phyir// dri med zla
4b3(1): gsal nyi zla'i 'od// dur khrod chen po'i dbyings na bzhugs// 'bar ba chen po'i klong na bzhugs// rigs ni rdo rje rigs kyi gtso// mun pa 'joms pa'i shes rab 'od// 'gro ba'i gnyen gcig ded dpon
4b4(1): gtso// 'gro ba'i dri ma sel ba'i skal// 'gro ba yongs kyi gnyen gcig gtso// gnyis med bde ba'i dbyings dkyil du// dgyes pa chen po dbab tu gsol// ho// zhes yum gyis mnyam pa'i ngang nas// de skad
4b5(1): ces gsungs so// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das dgyes pa chen po dur khrod kyi klong na/ gdug pa can gyi khri la zhabs mnyam pa'i skyil mo krung gi bzhugs nas/ rgyal po dga' ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la
4b6(1): snyoms par zhugs nas/ rdo rje'i tshig tu 'di skad ces glengs so// kye ma'o// rgyal bas 'gro don bya ba'i phyir// rigs kyi yum dang gnyis med par// pad+ma chen po brdeg tu gsol// 'khor rnams ma lus bskyed
5a1(1): gsol// zhes dgongs pa gnyis su med par bzhugs so// de nas yum chen mo nyid kyi bsam pa g.yos par gyur te// e ma ho// ston pa'i bstan par bstan pa'i phyir// 'khor ba 'dus pa'i ded
5a2(1): dpon gtso// dgyes pa'i rdo rje dbang po yis// gnyis med dgyes par gyur nas ni// gsang ba chen po char chen phob ho// sa ma ya ho// sa ma ya s+t+waM/ a nu rA ga yA mi/ a nu rA ga yA haM/ dzaHhUM baM hoH/ hUM hUM hUM/
5a3(1): de nas yab yum gnyis su med pa las/ khro bo dang / khro mo dang sprul pa dang yang sbrul bcas pa thams cad thon par gyur nas hUM hUM hUM phaT phaT phaT/ badz+ra kI la ya hUM phaT/ ces rdo rje phur pa drag po'i sgra byung nas/
5a4(1): 'jig rten gyi dregs pa spa bkong nas/ yang rang bzhin gnyis su med par mnyam pa nyid kyis bzhugs te/ sgyu ma lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyis bzhugs so// rdo rje khros pa rtsa ba'i rgyud las gleng bslang ba'i le'u ste
5a5(1): gnyis pa'o// // de ltar mnyam pa nyid kyi ngang du gnas pa las/ bdag tu rmongs pa dang / rtog pa la mngon par zhen pa'i dbang gis yang dag pa'i lam dang bral nas/ gab pa'i gsang ba ma rtogs par//
5a6(1): sbas pa'i gsang ba la mngon par 'chel nas/ rgyu dang 'bras bu la rmongs pas srid pa'i sa bon rtsub mor gyur nas/ rab tu tsha ba'i dmyal bar skyes so// tsha ba'i sdug bsngal gyis gdungs pas/ 'di bas kyang
5b1(1): shin tu grang na ci ma rung snyam pas/ shin tu grang ba'i nang du skyes te/ tsha ba dang grang ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams brgyud cing / bskal pa stong phrag bcu gnyis su myong ngo // de nas yang yan lag sna tshogs pa dang /
5b2(1): gdug pa'i lag cha sna tshogs pa dang / nad bzhi brgya rtsa bzhis 'debs par byed pa/ lha'i rigs dang lha ma yin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'bras bu che ba man chad dbang du bsdus so// bde bar gshegs pa thams
5b3(1): cad kyis mkhyen pas gzigs nas/ thugs rje'i byin gyis rlabs kyis/ de nas bde ba gshegs pa thams cad dgongs pa'i byin gyis rlabs gyis// de nas bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje gzhon nus/ bde bar
5b4(1): gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kyi sras su bskyed nas/ sras ni chos nyid skye ba med pa las/ 'jigs pa'i gzugs skur bzhengs pa'i phyir na sras// mchog ni de las bzhengs kyang g.yos pa med// sras ni ru
5b5(1): tra 'dul phyir bde gshegs byin gyis sras// mchog ni de las sbrul kyang g.yos pa med// sras ni skye med sras po rdo rje gzhon nu'i sku// mchog ni gang la gang 'dul mi bzad phur pa drug/ ces bde ba gshegs
5b6(1): pas byin gyi rlabs kyis bstod nas/ dbu gsum phyag drug zhabs bzhi pa gcig tu sprul nas/ hUM hUM hUM phaT phaT phaT ces khros pas lus po gcig la mgo bo brgyar sprul nas/ phyag na mtshon cha sna
6a1(1): tshogs pa bsnams pa/ 'khor ba thams cad bsdus nas/ shin tu 'gyings bag dang bcas par gyur te/ hi hi hi zhes shin tu nga rgyal dang bcas par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das sras mchog
6a2(1): nyid kyis/ dur khrod kyi klong na gdug pa can thams cad kyi gdan la bzhugs nas/ oM badz+ra kI li kikI la ya sarba big+h+nAM baM hUM phaT/ ces brjod pas shin tu rngam pa'i gzi brjid dang ldan par gyur
6a3(1): to// g.yas dkar g.yon dmar dbus mthing zhal gsum pa mche ba bcu gnyis shangs gsum pa/ ba spu gyen du 'khyil ba'o// phyag drug dang po rdo rje rtse dgu/ bar pas rtse lnga/ g.yon gyi dang po me dpung / bar pa
6a4(1): kha T+wAM rtse gsum/ tha ma gnyis kyis rdo rje phur bu 'dril ba/ dur khrod chas brgyad gsol ba// rdzu 'phrul gyi zhabs bzhir bzhugs pa/ rdo rje'i gshogs pas 'jig rten gyi khams gang ba// sku tshon gang bas lus
6a5(1): la gtams pa/ yum dang gnyis su med par gyur to// rdo rje khros pas zhe sdang gcod// mtshon chen sngon po 'bar ba yis// nam mkha'i dkyil na thigs par shar// srog gi go ru shar ba dang // snying gi go ru
6a6(1): bsgom par bya/ zhes gsungs so// de nas khro bo'i tshogs thams cad sprul pa las/ oM badz+ra kro d+ha hUM kA ra hUM/ gardza gardza hUM phaT/ ces steng du khro bo hUM kA ra dang / yum chen rdo rje sgra 'byin ma sprul pa'i phra men ma
6b1(1): phag gi mgo can dang / smig bu'i mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha bi dza ya hUM ha na ha na hUM phaT/ shar du khro bo chen po rnam par rgyal ba dang / yum rdo rje snyems ma sprul pa'i phra men ma stag gi mgo can dang / bya rgod kyi
6b2(1): mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha nI la daN+Da hUM da ha da ha hUM phaT/ shar lho'i mtshams su khro bo chen po dbyug pa sngon po dang / yum rdo rje sder mo sprul pa'i phra men ma g.yag gi mgo can dang / bya rog gi mgo can no// oM
6b3(1): badz+ra kro d+ha ya man+ta ka hUM pa tsa pa tsa hUM phaT/ lho'i phyogs su khro bo ya man+ta ka dang / yum rdo rje dur khrod ma/ sprul pa'i phra men ma sha ba'i mgo can dang / 'ug pa'i mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha Ar+ya a tsa la hUM ban+d+ha ban+d+ha
6b4(1): hUM phaT/ lho nub tu khro bo chen po mi g.yo mgon po dang / yum rdo rje gtun khung ma sprul pa'i phra men ma gzig gi mgo can dang / khwa ta'i mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha ha ya grI wa hUM hu lu hu lu hUM phaT/ nub tu khro bo
6b5(1): chen po rta mgrin dang / yum rdo rje gtum mo sprul pa'i phra men byi li'i mgo can dang / pu shud kyi mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha a pa ra dzi ta hU~M tiSh+Tha tiSh+Tha hUM phaT/ nub byang khro bo chen po gzhan gyis mi thub pa dang /
6b6(1): yum rdo rje mda' snyoms ma sprul pa'i phra men ma sbyang ki'i mgo can dang / khra'i mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha a mr-i ta kuN+Da li hUM ts+tshin+na ts+tshin+da hUM phaT/ byang du khro bo bdud rtsi 'khyil pa dang / yum rdo rje rlung
7a1(1): 'byin ma sprul pa'i phra men ma seng ge'i mgo can dang / pha wang gi mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha trai lo kya bi dza ya hUM phaT/ b+hin+da b+hin+da hUM phaT/ byang shar du khro bo chen po khams gsum rnam par rgyal ba
7a2(1): dang / yum rdo rje gsod byed ma sprul pa'i phra men dred kyi mgo can dang / sre mo'i mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha ma hA ba la hUM s+phoT s+pho Ta hUM phaT/ 'og tu khro bo chen po stobs po che dang / yum rdo rje bskyod byed ma dang /
7a3(1): sprul pa'i phra men ma dom gyi mgo can dang // byi ba'i mgo can gyis gtams pa'o// de rnams thams cad kyang 'thon par gyur te/ rab tu khros par gyur to// oM badz+ra kI li kI li ya hUM hUM hUM phaT phaT phaT/ ces
7a4(1): rab tu khros te/ stong gsum dus gcig tu g.yos te/ bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje gzhon nu 'khor bcas kyis gang bar gyur nas/ stong gsum dus gcig tu g.yos so// srin po chen po shin tu gdug pa dang
7a5(1): bcas pa bros te/ mi thub par 'chor ba la bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje gzhon du nyid kyis shin tu khros rab tu khros pa las/ mi bzad pa'i sras mchog rnam pa drug 'thon par gyur te/ ta thA ya ta thA ya hUM phaT/
7a6(1): ha sa ya ra ha sa ya ra hUM phaT/ shrI g+h+raM A na ya hUM phaT/ dza lA pa ya dza lA pa ya hUM phaT/ A we sha ya A we sha ya hUM phaT/ bin+d+ha ya bin+d+ha ya hUM phaT/ ces sras mchog rnam pa drug gis klong chen drug gi las byas te/ stod
7b1(1): ni zhal gsum phyag drug pa// smad ni zur gsum dpal dang ldan// khro mo bcu yis yongs brgyan nas// gdug pa ma lus bsgral bar bya'o// snying rjes bsgral ba'i dam tshig ni// bsad cing mnan pa ma yin
7b2(1): te// phung po rdo rjes gtams byas nas// rnam par shes pa rdo rjer bsgom// hUM hUM hUM kI li kI la ya zhes rab tu khros pas rang dbang chen po bskur te/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i rig 'dzin rnams// srid pa rdo rje 'grub
7b3(1): mdzod cig/ srid pa rdo rje phur bu'i lha// ye shes khro bor 'grub par mdzod// sangs rgyas kun gyi ye shes ni// ngang nyid rdo rje chos dbyings las// 'bar ba'i khro bo mi bzad pa// sku yi dbyig tu bdag skyed
7b4(1): cig/ thabs kyi spyod pas 'gro don du// byams dang snying rjes gang 'dul ba// sangs rgyas phrin las rdzogs mdzad nas// dbang dang byin rlabs bdag la stsol// srid pa'i phur bu bsgrub pa dang // dbang dang
7b5(1): dngos grub blang ba'i phyir// ye shes khro bo gshegs su gsol// khro bo chen po gshegs nas kyang // rtags dang mtshan ma bstan pa dang // kI la ya yi dngos grub stsol// zhes dbang bskur nas/ oM lam hUM lam
7b6(1): s+t+waM b+ha nan/ mo ha g+hA ta ya/ b+ha ga wAn/ shrI g+h+raM hriHSh+ThaHbi traM yang 'dug kyang rgyu mtshan dpyad/ bi kr-i badz+ra hUM ka ra hUM hUM phaT phaT/ badz+ra ki li ki la ya dzaHhUM baM hoH/ sarba big+h+nAM/ badz+ra kI li kI la ya hUM hUM phaT phaT/ hUM kA ra hUM
8a1(1): phaT/ badz+ra hUM kA ra hUM a/ stong gsum dus gcig tu g.yos nas/ khro bo chen po rnams ni sku che chung tshad ri rab tsam mo// mang nyung ni stong gi 'jig rten yungs 'brus bkang ba tsam du gyur nas/ oM
8a2(1): badz+ra kI li kI la ya hUM hUM hUM phaT phaT phaT/ ces rdo rje phur pa dril zhing sku bsigs nas/ dur khrod kyi klong na rab tu khros nas/ phyogs bcur gzigs pas/ mthu che ba'i dbang phyug chen po la sogs pa ma hA de wa
8a3(1): brgyal bar gyur/ rdo rje phur pa rab tu 'bar ba/ nyi zer la ser ba 'bab pa bzhin du btab pas/ kha T+wAM ga'i rtse la blangs pas de rab tu brgyal nas/ zong zong snying rje'i bdag po ci de ltar byed dam/ ma byed
8a4(1): shin tu gdug pa dang bcas nas smras pa las/ de ltar 'jig byed kyi dpal rdo rje gzhon nus phur pa byin gyis rlabs te/ cho ga gsum gyis skur bskyed nas// snyan gsan spyan drangs dbang nod nas// dbang
8a5(1): bskur thim gyur thob bsam nas// bcod brgyad sngags kyis gzi byin bskyed// rnam gsum tshul bzhin mchod pa dbul// phur pa bkrag dang gzi mdangs bskyed// byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed cing // dus
8a6(1): gsum rgyal ba'i gdung gsob pa'i// rig 'dzin bdag cag rnams la ni// gnod cing gdug pa'i dgra dang bgegs// bdud dang bar du gcod pa yi// dngos grub 'phrog cing 'tshe ba rnams// khro bo chen po'i
8b1(1): byin rlabs kyis// yud tsam gyis ni 'dir bkug nas// mngon sbyor tshul bzhin bsgral ba dang // lus ngag rdul du bshig nas kyang // sdug bsngal nyams su myong bar mdzod// oM lam hUM lam staM b+ha nan//
8b2(1): mo ha g+hA ta ya/ b+ha ga wAn/ shI g+h+raM bi kr-i badz+ra hUM kA ra hUM hUM phaT phaT/ oM badz+ra kI li ki la ya dzaHhUM baM hoH/ sarba big+h+nAM/ badz+ra ki li kI la ya hUM hUM phaT phaT badz+ra hUM ka ra hUM A/ thams cad phur bus btab nas shin
8b3(1): tu myos shing rid par gyur pa'i badz+ra yak+ka kro d+ha khA hi khA hi/ ha ha ha zhes snying dang nang khrol kun phyung nas/ yan lag kun gtubs nas/ sha zos khrag 'thungs rus pa kun 'chos nas/ hUM hUM hUM phaT phaT phaT/ ces
8b4(1): bden pa mthong nas 'bangs su mchi 'bangs su nan tan ma chung zhig/ shes pa bla med gnas su sbar// phung po dur khrod gnas bya zhing // gzugs phung nga yi stan bya'o// chos nyid kyi bden pa'o// gsang sngags
8b5(1): kyi byin gyis rlabs so// sangs rgyas kyi mthu'o// a b+hi tsar+ya'i dus la bab po// brnag pa de kho na la'o// zhes byin rlabs kyi gnang ba'o// rdo rje khros pa rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ drag po dregs pa can btul ba'i le'u
8b6(1): ste gsum pa'o// // de nas dregs pa 'dul byed gtso bo 'jig rten gyi dregs pa can rnams dngangs nas/ ye shes dang las la grub pa'i ma mos kyang srog gi snying po phul nas/ dpa' bo chen po 'khor
9a1(1): bcas la// bdag cag rnams kyang 'bangs su mchi// yang bud med nag mo khrag gi ral pa can gyis kyang / bdag gi srog gi snying po 'di// dpa' bo chen pos bzhes su gsol// de nas yang bud
